# dialer.py

class Dialer:
    def __init__(self):
        self.teams_integration = TeamsIntegration()
        self.excel_reader = ExcelReader()
        self.audio_player = AudioPlayer()

    def automate_calling_from_excel(self, excel_file):
        phone_numbers = self.excel_reader.read_excel(excel_file)
        for phone_number in phone_numbers:
            self.teams_integration.call_number(phone_number)
            self.audio_player.play_audio("ringtone.mp3")

class TeamsIntegration:
    def call_number(self, phone_number):
        # Logic to call a phone number using Microsoft Teams
        pass

    def read_excel(self, excel_file):
        # Logic to read phone numbers from an Excel file
        pass

class AudioPlayer:

        # Logic to play audio file
        pass
